print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

            break

        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

import socket

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

HOST = (socket.gethostname(), 1000)
filename = "file_client.txt"
chunk = 2

client = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
client.connect(HOST)
print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()

print(f"Connected to {HOST}")

with open(filename, "wb") as file:
    while True:
        message = client.recv(chunk)
        if message == b"":
            break
        print(message)
        file.write(message)

client.close()
